#Random Events

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Ids assigned are in format
# Category: 2 digits
# Version:  2 digits - incremental for same category, type and group, starting at 00
# Type:     1 digit
# Group:    3 digits - Range: 000 - 999 - First free: 125
#
# Category                Comment
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# 90   countrysize   1    Minors
# 91   countrysize   4    Big minors
# 92   countrysize   9    Majors
# 93   countrysize  30    Big majors/colonial powers
# 94   countrysize  80    Superpowers
# 95   countrysize 200    Continent-spanning empires
# 96   general            Non-staggered events
#
# Type    Event set
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
# 0       Unreserved
# 8       AI events
# 9       Human events


#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Dummy - Set of 20 events for MUS (the Pope) tag only
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96008000
	trigger = {
		owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } #Dummy province

	random = yes
	name = "AI_EVENT"
	desc = ""
	#-#Dummy

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Random Revolt
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 92000000 #Paradox 1001
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM000" #Unprovoked Revolts
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM000"
	#-#Revolts were almost part of everyday life for the rulers all over Europe. High taxes noblemen cruelties as well as cultural and religious differencies caused unhappiness among the farmers and in the cities and in the most extreme cases this led to rebellions with sometimes long lasting and drastic effect.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 93000000 #Paradox 1001
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 30
		NOT = { countrysize = 80 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM000" #Unprovoked Revolt
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM000"
	#-#Revolts were almost part of everyday life for the rulers all over Europe. High taxes noblemen cruelties as well as cultural and religious differencies caused unhappiness among the farmers and in the cities and in the most extreme cases this led to rebellions with sometimes long lasting and drastic effect.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Religious Turmoil
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 92008001 #Paradox 1002
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		year = 1530
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = asia
		}
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM001" #Religious Turmoil
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM001"
	#-#After the Reformation, the European continent would have to live for several hundred years with religious differences causing rebellions and uprisings more or less frequently.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM001A" #Crush the revolt
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM001B" #Grant them limited autonomy
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM001C" #Use this to eliminate some heathens
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = conversion which = -3 }
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -3 }
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -3 }
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -3 }
		command = { type = population which = -3 value = -5000 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Conversion of Heretics
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000002 #Paradox 1003
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM002" #Conversion of Heretics
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM002"
	#-#Religious policy almost always supported by the might of Royal power was often directed at eradicating heresy. This led to massive, if not willing, conversions of the people regarded as heretics by the religious leadership.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = conversion which = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96010002 #Paradox 6501
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { domestic = { type = INNOVATIVE value = 3 } }
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM002" #Conversion of Heretics
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM002"
	#-#Religious policy almost always supported by the might of Royal power was often directed at eradicating heresy. This led to massive, if not willing, conversions of the people regarded as heretics by the religious leadership.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = conversion which = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Gift To the State
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000003 #Paradox 1004
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM003" #Gift to the State
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM003"
	#-#Good governments would sometimes prompt the nobility and the businessmen of the realm to donate cash to the treasury, out of pure patriotism or in exchange for the sales or transfer of honorary titles and positions.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = treasury value = 50 }
	}
}

	}

	random = yes

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Scandal at the Court
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000004 #Paradox 1007
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM004" #Scandal at the Court
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM004"
	#-#Sometimes a scandal would erupt in the royal court and would upset a monarch to the point where most diplomatic activity would come to a standstill until things quieted down a bit.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM004A" #Do nothing
		command = { type = DIP which = -2 value = 6 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -10 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM004B" #Toss some money around to cover things up
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM004C" #Twist this to our advantage
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = DIP which = -2 value = 30 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -45 }
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -3 value = 12 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Wave of Obscurantism
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96009005 #Paradox 1008
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		NOT = { event = 103 } #Global: Edict of Tolerance
		continent = europe
		OR = {
			religion = Catholic
			religion = Counterreform
			religion = Protestant
			religion = Reformed
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM005" #Wave of Obscurantism
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM005"
	#-#As a typical response to different kinds of problems obscurantism was a frequent behavior in most nations at least until the Age of Enlightenment arose in the most advanced western nations of the European continent.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005A" #Do nothing
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = serfdom value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005B" #Give support to local efforts
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005C" #React harshly
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = missionaries value = -2 }
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 5 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
	}
	action_d = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005D" #Encourage it
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = missionaries value = 2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96008005 #Paradox 1008
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = yes
		NOT = { event = 103 } #Global: Edict of Tolerance
		continent = europe
		OR = {
			religion = Catholic
			religion = Counterreform
			religion = Protestant
			religion = Reformed
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM005" #Wave of Obscurantism
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM005"
	#-#As a typical response to different kinds of problems obscurantism was a frequent behavior in most nations at least until the Age of Enlightenment arose in the most advanced western nations of the European continent.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005A" #Do nothing
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = serfdom value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM005B" #Give support to local efforts
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Exceptional Year
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000006 #Paradox 1009
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = 2
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM006" #Exceptional Year
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM006"
	#-#Excellent business environment combined with good harvests were once in a while a blessing for the nation's tax base generating higher income for the realm.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM006A" #Add the excess revenue to the treasury
		command = { type = treasury value = 100 }
		command = { type = inflation value = -2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM006B" #Reinvest it in the local economy
		command = { type = provincetax which = -1 value = 1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM006C" #Use the excess revenue to expand commerce
		command = { type = infra value = 100 }
		command = { type = trade value = 100 }
	}
	action_d = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM006D" #Use the excess revenue for military needs
		command = { type = land value = 100 }
		command = { type = naval value = 100 }
	}
}

	id = 91000007 #Paradox 1010
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1550
		continent = europe
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM007" #Rush of Colonists
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM007"
	#-#Demographic, economic and political pressure at home made way for sudden increases in the number of people looking for a better life in rich uncharted lands and businessmen in search of adventure and wealth in overseas trade.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = colonists value = 1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000008 #Paradox 1011
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM008" #Diplomatic Move
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM008"
	#-#Diplomacy between nations was often affected by random factors from both sides involved that were most of the time beyond the control of the foreign ministers involved.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = DIP which = 1 value = 4 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 25 }
		command = { type = diplomats value = 1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91000009 #Paradox 1012
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { badboy = 40 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM009" #Great Reputation
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM009"
	#-#Diplomacy between nations was often affected by the fame and numerous other achievements of a nation. Her diplomats would capitalize on those factors to achieve better results than usual in their negotiations.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = DIP which = 1 value = 24 }
		command = { type = diplomats value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 10 }
	}
}

	id = 96000010 #Paradox 1014
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 }
		infra = 3
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
		NOT = { religion = pagan }
		countrysize = 4
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM010" #Unexpected Invention
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM010"
	#-#Unexpected inventions sometimes led to immediate technical applications, and manufactories were built to exploit them.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = gainmanufactory which = -1 value = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Unexpected Invention (Confusician)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#(Neo-)confucian stressed, more than any other religion/philosophy
#ar the time, stability over change. New innovations brought change
#which ultimately leads to instability. That is why confucian
#countries get special innovation event

event = {
	id = 96039010 #Paradox 1014
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 }
		infra = 3
		religion = confucian
		countrysize = 4
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM010" #Unexpected Invention
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM010"
	#-#Unexpected inventions sometimes led to immediate technical applications, and manufactories were built to exploit them.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM010A" #Ignore the Invention
		command = { type = ADM which = 1 value = 12 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
		command = { type = vp value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM010B" #Embrace the new idea!
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = ADM which = -2 value = 12 }
		command = { type = gainmanufactory which = -1 value = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96049010 #Paradox 1014
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 7 }
		infra = 3
		religion = confucian
		countrysize = 4

	random = yes

	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM010"

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM010A" #Ignore the Invention
		command = { type = ADM which = 1 value = 12 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
		command = { type = vp value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM010B" #Embrace the new idea!
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = ADM which = -2 value = 12 }

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Rush of Merchants
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000011 #Paradox 1015
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM011" #Rush of Merchants
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM011"
	#-#Maritime trade expansion led to a growing desire among merchants to start new shipping and trade ventures on the high seas.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Plague (Pre-Columbian Non-Americas)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#Note: These events have been done as such to represent the Americas
#relative isolation from most major diseases of the world at the time
#Columbus came to America. This wasn't to say the America's were without
#there deadly diseases, as is shown by increased death toll among euro-
#peans after 1st major contact with the new land represents, but that
#there relative isolation acted as both a barrier prior to Columbus
#(reducing the severity and number of major plagues) as well as making
#them woefully underprepared for the new European carried diseases.
#Thus they get a break early on, but later get the worse end.
#
#These will be the only events that have double copies (same event, same
#triggers, 2 ids) because of the nature of the events to show the
#disproportiante number of plagues in an area.

event = {
	id = 90000012 #Paradox 1016
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { year = 1550 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		NOT = { continent = america }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM012" #Plague
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM012"
	#-#Epidemics in the early-modern era were far deadlier than wars or even famine. Diseases that with modern medicine are relatively harmless like smallpox or flu took a heavy toll whenever they struck especially among infants.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = -1000 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90030012 #Paradox 1016
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1550
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		OR = {
			NOT = { continent = america }
			AND = {
				continent = america
				NOT = { religion = pagan }
			}
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM012" #Plague
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM012"
	#-#Epidemics in the early-modern era were far deadlier than wars or even famine. Diseases that with modern medicine are relatively harmless like smallpox or flu took a heavy toll whenever they struck especially among infants.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = -1500 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91030012 #Paradox 1016
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
		year = 1550
		OR = {
			NOT = { continent = america }
			AND = {
				continent = america
				NOT = { religion = pagan }
			}
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM012" #Plague
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM012"
	#-#Epidemics in the early-modern era were far deadlier than wars or even famine. Diseases that with modern medicine are relatively harmless like smallpox or flu took a heavy toll whenever they struck especially among infants.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = -1500 }
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = -1500 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90040012 #Paradox 1016
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1550
		NOT = { year = 1650 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		continent = america
		religion = pagan
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM012" #Plague
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM012"
	#-#Epidemics in the early-modern era were far deadlier than wars or even famine. Diseases that with modern medicine are relatively harmless like smallpox or flu took a heavy toll whenever they struck especially among infants.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = -2000 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90000013 #Paradox 1017
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		domestic = { type = land value = 5 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		NOT = { land = 60 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM013" #Reformation of the Army
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM013"
	#-#Army reformation be it from new tactics weapons or command or any other reason often translated into better combat efficiency.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = land value = 250 }
	}
}

	}

event = {
	id = 90000018 #Paradox 1023
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { stability = 3 }
		NOT = { trade = 10 }
		NOT = { infra = 10 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM018" #Good Government Policies
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM018"
	#-#Changes of policies when cleverly timed and made were often well perceived by the people of the time beyond their actual efficiency as a proof of the government's good will and interest in the welfare of the realm.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = infra value = 100 }
		command = { type = trade value = 100 }
	}
}

	id = 92000019 #Paradox 1024
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { trade = 10 }
		NOT = { infra = 10 }
		countrysize = 9
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM019" #Poor Government Policies
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM019"
	#-#Changes of policies when poorly timed and made were often wrongly perceived by the people of the time beyond their actual efficiency as a proof of the government ill will and lack of interest in the welfare of the realm.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = infra value = -400 }
		command = { type = trade value = -400 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 92008020 #Paradox 1025
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		stability = -2
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM020" #Unhappiness among the Clergy
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM020"
	#-#Conflict of opinion or interest over religious or secular matters between the ruler and the religious authorities often upset the clergy, which used its strong preaching power to influence the people of the realm.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM020A" #Ignore their Demands
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM020B" #Agree to their Demands
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90000021 #Paradox 1026
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		domestic = { type = serfdom value = 2 }
		NOT = { infra = 10 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM021" #Unhappiness among the Artisans
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM021"
	#-#Conflict and protests over taxes corporations trade and customs policies were quite frequent and could result in sharp drops in industrial production.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM021A" #Execute the Troublemakers
		command = { type = infra value = -100 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM021B" #Abolish a Tax
		command = { type = domestic which = serfdom value = -1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
	}
}

	id = 96000034 #Paradox 1040
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		naval = 11
		trade = 3
		NOT = { domestic = { type = land value = 5 } }
		NOT = { religion = pagan }
		year = 1601
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM022" #Explorer
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM022"
	#-#A bold captain has put himself his ship and his crew at our disposal to win glory for God and country! The vast tract of still unknown sea lanes and unexplored lands would always attract seamen in search of adventure fame and wealth.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = explorer which = -1 }
		command = { type = colonists value = 2 }
	}
}

	}

	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM023"

		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Agricultural Revolution
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 91000024 #Paradox 1021
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM024" #Agricultural Revolution
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM024"
	#-#New farming techniques plantations irrigation and land properties organization were soon translated into increased agricultural production and therefore higher tax income for the state. However countries with backward peasantry and conservative political structure were slower than others to put progress into effect.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = provincemanpower which = -1 value = 1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90009025 #Paradox 1028
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM025" #Unhappiness among the Merchants
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM025"
	#-#Conflict and protests over taxes corporations port duties navy requisitions trade and customs policies were quite frequent and often had counterproductive effects.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM025A" #Refuse to change our position
		command = { type = merchants value = -1 }
		command = { type = trade value = -100 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM025B" #Agree to some of their demands
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
		command = { type = domestic which = mercantilism value = -1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM025C" #Use this as an excuse to seize their assets!
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = trade value = -200 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 50 }
		command = { type = merchants value = -6 }
		command = { type = domestic which = mercantilism value = 1 }
	}
}

	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM025"
	#-#Conflict and protests over taxes corporations port duties navy requisitions trade and customs policies were quite frequent and often had counterproductive effects.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM025A" #Refuse to change our position
		command = { type = merchants value = -1 }
		command = { type = trade value = -300 }
	}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#New Mineral in Mine
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000026 #Paradox 1029
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		OR = {
			NOT = { continent = america }
			AND = {
				continent = america
				year = 1600
			}
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM026" #New vein discovered
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM026"
	#-#Discoveries of new veins of precious metals sometimes increased the value of a mine significantly.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = mine which = -1 value = 10 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Political Crisis
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000027 #Paradox 1030
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM027" #Political Crisis
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM027"
	#-#Political crises may occur from time to time. They may involve a conflict between the ruler and the parliament or unrest among the nobility or conflicts of interest between the nobility and the merchants or religious leaders. In game terms these problems usually cause a loss of stability when they occur.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM027A" #Don't take sides
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = ADM which = -2 value = 6 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM027B" #Side with one faction
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96010027 #Paradox 1030

		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Corruption, 2 sets
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000028 #Paradox 1031
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM028" #Corruption
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM028"
	#-#Corruption is one of the most common and frequent factors of political and economic life as always but all the more so in feudal regimes.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM028A" #Try to eradicate the problems
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM028B" #Ignore them
		command = { type = inflation value = 1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91000028 #Paradox 1031
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM028" #Corruption
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM028"
	#-#Corruption is one of the most common and frequent factors of political and economic life as always but all the more so in feudal regimes.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM028A" #Try to eradicate the problems
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -75 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM028B" #Ignore them
		command = { type = inflation value = 1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Deflation
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000029 #Paradox 1032
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM029" #Deflation
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM029"
	#-#Rampant inflation originating from the vast inflow of silver and gold from the new world brought the Kingdom of Spain to bankruptcy in 1557 and 1597. However economic cycles led to reduction of inflation a process called deflation.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = inflation value = -2 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Diplomatic Insult
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000030 #Paradox 1033
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM030" #Diplomatic Insult
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM030"
	#-#Conflicts sometimes erupted following diplomatic insults.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -1 value = 6 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -10 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -10 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91000031 #Paradox 1034
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		infra = 3
		countrysize = 6
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM031" #Fortification Effort
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM031"
	#-#A permanent matter of regal attention fortification of the realm always received great care, particularly at the border or in strategic places such as capitals major shipyards or important colonies.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = fortress which = -1 value = 1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Bank (Non-Asian)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#Banks were in China and other areas of the East long before they were in Europe.

event = {
	id = 90000032 #Paradox 1035
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1650
		domestic = { type = centralization value = 3 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		NOT = { religion = pagan }
		infra = 7
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM032" #Creation of Bank
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM032"
	#-#The creation of a centralized state bank brought serious improvement to the economic life of a country, as it helped stabilize the currency and regulate the state budgets.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = inflation value = -3 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 75 }
	}
}

	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM032" #Creation of Bank
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM032"
	#-#The creation of a centralized state bank brought serious improvement to the economic life of a country, as it helped stabilize the currency and regulate the state budgets.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = inflation value = -3 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 500 }
	}
}

#Stock Exchange
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#Stock Exchanges are IMO a decidely western invention. Even with the
#knowledge and abilitiy to do so, I dounbt if any nation outside a eurocentric
#one would have created anything like a stock exchange.

event = {
	id = 90000033 #Paradox 1036
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1750
		infra = 7
		trade = 9
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
			religion = protestant
			religion = reformed
		}
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = america
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM033" #Creation of Stock Exchange
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM033"
	#-#The creation of a Stock Exchange paved the way for the early forms of capitalism and signaled the start of easier access to financing, thereby improving the economic life of a country.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = inflation value = -2 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 25 }
		command = { type = infra value = 250 }
	}
}

#Company of Trade
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#Again, like the Stock Exchange, Company's of Trade are a western invention.
#While similar entities of private/public ownership existed in
#many regions they in no way were close to what this event seeks to describe.

event = {
	id = 90000034 #Paradox 1037
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1650
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
			religion = protestant
			religion = reformed
		}
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = america
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM034" #Creation of Company of Trade
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM034"
	#-#The creation of a Company of Trade was usually a boost to a country's economy, attracting more capital and people to overseas business ventures!

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = merchants value = 1 }
		command = { type = trade value = 250 }
	}
}

	trigger = {

		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}

	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM035" #Colonial Uprising
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM035"
	#-#From time to time the colonists rebelled due to high taxes or duties lack of attention or cruel Governors. Similarly white men's oppression led to outbursts of native rebellion or slave revolts.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = colonialrevolt which = -1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 92000036 #Paradox 1039
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 6 } }
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM036" #Heretics
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM036"
	#-#Despite various official religious policies to eradicate heresy the population of some provinces was sometimes strongly attached to their faith and resisted conversion. Similarly, new faiths would also engage in missionary activity and manage to convert whole regions to their own belief.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -1 }
		command = { type = religiousrevolt which = -1 }
	}
}

#Nobles

event = {
	id = 96000037 #Paradox 1042
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 10 } }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM037" #Nobles demand recovery of former rights
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM037"
	#-#The privileges of the nobility were continually under assault as the monarch tried to centralize more and more control. Sometimes the nobles would attempt to gain rights they had lost or surrendered to the monarch in earlier times.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM037A" #Accept their rightful claims
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM037B" #Execute the Traitors
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = -1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM037C" #Ignore the demands
		command = { type = revoltrisk which = 24 value = 2 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Trading Company Disaster
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#Just like many things, these are western ideas and likely would not originate elsewhere.

event = {
	id = 90000038 #Paradox 1043
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1700
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
			religion = protestant
			religion = reformed
		}
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = america
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM038" #Trading Company Bubble Bursts
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM038"
	#-#Trading companies were often founded on highly speculative stocks. When they failed, large sums of wealth could be lost and faith in the goverment declined as well.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
		command = { type = trade value = -250 }
	}
}

	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM040" #Meteor Sighted
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM040"
	#-#The peasants were always superstitious, and the appearance of a meteor in the sky could cause panic among the people. This was often viewed as a sign that the end of times were near or that something bad would happen in the near future.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = revoltrisk value = 1 }
	}
}

		command = { type = revoltrisk value = -1 }
	}

		command = { type = revoltrisk value = -1 }
	}

		infra = 3
	}

	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM045"

	}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Noble Feud
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 91000046 #Paradox 1049
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 4 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM046" #Noble Families Feud
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM046"
	#-#Violence among leading families within a state was never far from the surface. Often, this instability would boil over into open confilict. The result was less than a full blown civil war but could immensely disturb the stability of a state.
	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046A" #Side with one family
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046B" #Let them fight it out.
		command = { type = stability value = -3 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046C" #Try to settle the issue.
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 92000046 #Paradox 1049
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 4 }
		countrysize = 9
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}

	#-#Violence among leading families within a state was never far from the surface. Often, this instability would boil over into open confilict. The result was less than a full blown civil war but could immensely disturb the stability of a state.
	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046A" #Side with one family
		command = { type = revolt which = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046B" #Let them fight it out.

	}

		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM046C" #Try to settle the issue.
		command = { type = treasury value = -100 }
	}
}

	}

	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM047" #Nobles Ally with Foreign Power
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM047"
	#-#The nobility was not fully subjugated during this age and the nobles could and did strike independent alliances with foreign princes. The crowns of Europe might not have liked it but they were normally hard pressed to prevent these kinds of activities.

		name = "OK"

		command = { type = casusbelli which = -1 value = 24 }
	}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Cessation of Church Functions to Nobility
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000049 #Paradox 1052
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
			religion = orthodox
		}
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM049" #Cessation of Church Functions to Nobility
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM049"
	#-#Noble families were often granted control over church lands and appointment in many states in exchange for cash contributions to the crown's efforts. The crown, of course, lost control over some revenues this way in exhange for a short term boost in revenue.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM049A" #Decline
		command = { type = vp value = -5 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM049B" #Accept
		command = { type = provincetax which = -1 value = -1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 100 }
	}
}

	id = 91000049 #Paradox 1052
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)

			religion = counterreform

		}
		countrysize = 4
	}
	random = yes

	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM049"

		command = { type = vp value = -5 }
	}

	id = 90000050 #Paradox 1053
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM050" #Sale of Offices
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM050"
	#-#The crown often resorted to short term cash grabs like the sale of government offices. These sales would bring in a lot of revenue but in the long haul more officials meant more tax revenue siphoned off before it reached the royal treasury.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM050A" #Decline
		command = { type = vp value = -5 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM050B" #Accept
		command = { type = provincetax which = -1 value = -1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 100 }
	}

	id = 90000051 #Paradox 1054
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		trade = 3
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM051" #Monopoly Company Formed
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM051"
	#-#Crowns often granted trading companies the exclusive rights to traffic in goods in a region. These monopolies were granted in exchange for a lump-sum payment and continuing revenues from the traders.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = merchants value = 1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 50 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Nobles Demand Increased Pensions
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000052 #Paradox 1055
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 7 } }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM052" #Nobles Demand Increased Pensions
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM052"
	#-#Kings had to keep their unruly nobles in line through many methods. One of the most common was cold hard cash. Nobles would demand increased pensions in exchange for relinquishing certain rights to the King.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM052A" #Refuse their demands
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM052B" #Accept their demands
		command = { type = treasury value = -75 }
	}
}

	id = 91000052 #Paradox 1055

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		countrysize = 9
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 7 } }
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM052" #Nobles Demand Increased Pensions
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM052"
	#-#Kings had to keep their unruly nobles in line through many methods. One of the most common was cold hard cash. Nobles would demand increased pensions in exchange for relinquishing certain rights to the King.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM052B" #Accept their demands
		command = { type = treasury value = -200 }
	}

event = {
	id = 96000056 #Paradox 1059
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 10 } }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = centralization value = 2 } }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM056" #Nobles Demand Old Rights
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM056"
	#-#The nobility during this period still recalled the days when the King was just the first among many nobles. The nobility wanted to return to these days and would frequently pressure the King to regain certain lost rights of privileges.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM056A" #Reject Demands
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM056B" #Accept Demands
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = 1 }
	}
}

	id = 96000057 #Paradox 1060
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		countrysize = 4
		domestic = { type = centralization value = 2 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM057" #Cities Demand Old Rights
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM057"
	#-#Urban dwellers had always existed under a different code of rules than their rural brethren - even in the same state. Just as monarchs looked to curb the privileges of nobles they often tried to bring cities under more uniform rules and regulations. The cities often resisted these efforts.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM057A" #Deny Old Rights
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM057B" #Accept
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Non-enforcement of Ordinances
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000058 #Paradox 1061
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		domestic = { type = centralization value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = centralization value = 10 } }
		}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM058" #Non-enforcement of Ordinances
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM058"
	#-#Monarchs ruled by issuing ordinances but they were almost powerless to enforce them. Enforcement depended upon the local powers (nobles/city governments) who would not always be as vigilant as the monarchs would have desired.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM058A" #Enforce it
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM058B" #Ignore it
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = -1 }
	}
}

	id = 96000059 #Paradox 1062
	trigger = {

		trade = 2
		domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 10 } }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM059" #Bourgeoisie Request Privileges
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM059"
	#-#The Bourgeoisie class grew increasing resentful of the power of the noble families and particularly their lack of opportunities in the higher ranks of government. One route into power was to marry into poor but well titled noble families. The other was to pry open positions in government circles.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM059A" #Grant
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM059B" #Deny
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = 1 }
	}
}

#Italian Engineer Available

event = {
	id = 91000060 #Paradox 1063
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1450
		NOT = { year = 1600 }
		continent = europe
		domestic = { type = offensive value = 3 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 9	}
 	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM060" #Italian Engineer Available
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM060"
	#-#During the period from 1450-1600 Italian siege engineers were highly sought after to teach the ways of the trace italienne to the militaries of Europe. These engineers had no national identity in most cases and simply worked for whoever could afford to pay them.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM060A" #Decline the Offer
		command = { type = vp value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM060B" #Hire the engineer
		command = { type = treasury value = -75 }
		command = { type = domestic which = offensive value = -1 }
		command = { type = fortress which = -1 value = 1 }
	}
}

		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1450
		NOT = { year = 1600 }
		continent = europe
		domestic = { type = offensive value = 3 }
		countrysize = 30
		NOT = { countrysize = 80 }
 	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM060" #Italian Engineer Available
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM060"
	#-#During the period from 1450-1600 Italian siege engineers were highly sought after to teach the ways of the trace italienne to the militaries of Europe. These engineers had no national identity in most cases and simply worked for whoever could afford to pay them.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM060B" #Hire the engineer

		command = { type = domestic which = offensive value = -1 }
		command = { type = fortress which = -1 value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM060A" #Decline the Offer
		command = { type = vp value = -10 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91000061 #Paradox 1064
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		continent = europe
		NOT = { domestic = { type = offensive value = 10 } }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = quality value = 10 } }
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM061" #Foreign Drill Instructor Available
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM061"
	#-#Maurice of Orange pioneered new drills for firearms that made the new weapons much more effective. This drill technique was not a secret and numerous military entrepreneurs read on the drill and placed their service at the disposal of the crowned heads of Europe.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM061A" #Decline the Offer
		command = { type = vp value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM061B" #Hire him
		command = { type = treasury value = -250 }
		command = { type = domestic which = offensive value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = quality value = 1 }
		command = { type = INF which = -1 value = 1000 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Build a Great Palace
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 92009062 #Paradox 1065
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		atwar = no
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { domestic = { type = aristocracy value = 10 } }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = centralization value = 10 } }
		infra = 1
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM062" #Build a Great Palace
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM062"
	#-#Monarchs struggles with ways to subdue the nobility. The rise of firearms reduced the nobles' role as warriors but left them with in the eyes of the monarchs too much idle time. Some monarchs created great new palaces with elaborate court rituals to dazzle the nobles and keep them occupied. Versailles is the greatest expression of this movement.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM062A" #Don't build it
		command = { type = vp value = -50 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM062B" #Build the Palace
		command = { type = treasury value = -500 }
		command = { type = domestic which = aristocracy value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = 1 }
		command = { type = vp value = 25 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96000063 #Paradox 1066
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		countrysize = 4
		religion = catholic
		NOT = { year = 1514 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM063" #Indulgence peddler in our domain
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM063"
	#-#Indulgences were essentially a pre-pay system for our sins. A devotee could buy forgiveness before they committed sins. This practice was widely practiced and its abuse was one of the prompts for Luther's movement. Indulgence peddlers were very apt at extracting large amounts of cash from any area they passed through.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = provincetax which = -1 value = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Uncooperative Philosopher
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96009064 #Paradox 1067
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 10 } }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM064" #Uncooperative Philosopher
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM064"
	#-#Many times men of ideas would posit ideas that ran counter to accept doctrine either from the monarch or the church. The state would normally try to get the thinker to recant his ideas and, failing that, would resort to imprisonment or execution. Men like Giordono Bruno, Thomas Moore and Galileo are classic examples of troublesome thinkers.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM064A" #Imprison Thinker
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM064B" #Allow to Remain Free
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
	}
}

	random = yes
	trigger = {

		stability = -2
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM065" #Regional Heresy
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM065"
	#-#Small bouts of heretical ideas would spring up from time to time. Most were simple people who did not realize that their interpretation of the Bible went counter to established doctrine but all such ideas frightened the local rulers. Intended or not, the usual response was quick and brutal as authorities would suppress these outbreaks.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM065A" #Ignore Heresy
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM065B" #Fund suppression effort
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Boundary Dispute
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 91000066 #Paradox 1069
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { stability = 3 }
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM066" #Boundary Dispute
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM066"
	#-#The lack of good maps or the tools to create accurate maps would occasionally lead to overlapping claims of authority in border regions. These disputes were usually over very marginal areas but could serve as a point of friction when monarchs decided to press the issue.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM066A" #Press Issue
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -1 value = 6 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM066B" #Settle Issue
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = 40 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 92000066 #Paradox 1069
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { stability = 3 }
		countrysize = 9
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM066" #Boundary Dispute
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM066"
	#-#The lack of good maps or the tools to create accurate maps would occasionally lead to overlapping claims of authority in border regions. These disputes were usually over very marginal areas but could serve as a point of friction when monarchs decided to press the issue.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM066B" #Settle Issue
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 40 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM066A" #Press Issue
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -3 value = 6 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -25 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Merchants Harassed
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000067 #Paradox 1070
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM067" #Merchants Harassed
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM067"
	#-#Disputes over the treatment of local merchants were not uncommon. All governments faced minor reports of unfair treatment and harassment of their merchants. At the higher levels there were complaints about banditry or privateering occuring within or at the direction of a certain state. These issues could be resolved but saber rattling was always an option.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM067A" #Escalate Complaint
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -1 value = 60 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM067B" #Diplomatically Resolve
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = 50 }
		command = { type = trade value = -100 }
	}
}

At the higher levels there were complaints about banditry or privateering occuring within or at the direction of a certain state. These issues could be resolved but saber rattling was always an option.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM067A" #Escalate Complaint
		command = { type = casusbelli which = -1 value = 60 }
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM067B" #Diplomatically Resolve
		command = { type = relation which = -3 value = 50 }
		command = { type = trade value = -1000 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Regional Population Boom (Europe/American)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000068 #Paradox 1071
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1550
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
			religion = protestant
			religion = reformed
		}
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = america
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM068" #Regional Population Boom
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM068"
	#-#A sudden baby boom was not always a blessing at this time. Agricultural societies could not easily scale to handle larger populations in a given region. Population pressures often led to efforts at immigration overseas or movement to the city.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM068A" #Grant Colonial Charter
		command = { type = colonists value = 3 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM068B" #Deny Charter
		command = { type = population which = -1 value = 2500 }
	}
}

#Regional Population Boom (Elsewhere)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

	id = 96010068 #Paradox 1071
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		year = 1550
		NOT = { countrysize = 30 }
		OR = {
			religion = sunni
			religion = shia
			religion = buddhist
			religion = confucian
			religion = pagan
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM068" #Regional Population Boom
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM068"
	#-#A sudden baby boom was not always a blessing at this time. Agricultural societies could not easily scale to handle larger populations in a given region. Population pressures often led to efforts at immigration overseas or movement to the city.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM068B" #Deny Charter
		command = { type = population which = -2 value = 2500 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM068A" #Grant Colonial Charter
		command = { type = colonists value = 3 }
	}
}

	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM069" #Great Noble Family Requests Aid
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM069"
	#-#The most powerful of the noble families in the state often had vast wealth but that did not stop them like their monarchs from getting into financial troubles. They too could accumulate debts that escaped their ability to pay. They could at those times come to the monarch to request aid. The monarchs were often receptive since they would usually be related by blood or marriage.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM069A" #Deny Aid
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM069B" #Grant Aid
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Support for Dissidents Abroad
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90000070 #Paradox 1074
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM070" #Support for Dissidents Abroad
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM070"
	#-#Monarchs were contacted by a variety of dissidents from other states. These dissidents claimed to have vast supporters who just needed some cash - they were usually lying. Despite this, their claims excited many influential people at the court - particularly when religion entered the mix. Supporting these dissidents rarely accomplished anything other than antagonizing the other state but failure to support could create a bad impression at home.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM070A" #Decline
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM070B" #Support
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -25 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 91000070 #Paradox 1074
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -2
		countrysize = 4
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM070" #Support for Dissidents Abroad
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM070"
	#-#Monarchs were contacted by a variety of dissidents from other states. These dissidents claimed to have vast supporters who just needed some cash - they were usually lying. Despite this, their claims excited many influential people at the court - particularly when religion entered the mix. Supporting these dissidents rarely accomplished anything other than antagonizing the other state but failure to support could create a bad impression at home.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM070B" #Support
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -25 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM070A" #Decline
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Foreign Trade Competition Rises
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 90009071 #Paradox 1075
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		domestic = { type = mercantilism value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = mercantilism value = 10 } }
		NOT = { trade = 10 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM071" #Foreign Trade Competition Rises
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM071"
	#-#Trade was heavily regulated during this era but despite this the markets were not fixed. At times merchants would try to enter new markets or sell new goods. Merchants facing these conditions would usually demand new or higher tariffs to stop their competitors.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM071A" #Impose New Tariff
		command = { type = domestic which = mercantilism value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM071B" #Deny New Tariff
		command = { type = domestic which = mercantilism value = -1 }
		command = { type = trade value = -100 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 90009072 #Paradox 1076
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 10 } }
		NOT = { countrysize = 4 }
		OR = {
			continent = europe
			continent = asia
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM072" #Exceptional Court Painter Available
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM072"
	#-#Courts were often looking for painters and artists to try to adequately capture the glory of the monarch. Artists during the Renaissance were usually multi-talented and worked in many fields other than art. Michelangelo worked in fortifications and da Vinci dabbled in engineering for example.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM072A" #Decline his Services
		command = { type = vp value = -1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM072B" #Hire Painter
		command = { type = treasury value = -25 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
		command = { type = vp value = 1 }
	}
}

		OR = {
			religion = sunni
			religion = shia
			religion = buddhist
			religion = confucian
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM073" #Chartering of a University
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM073"
	#-#Our advisors recommend that we charter a new University to support science and development. Should we heed their advise?

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM073A" #No
		command = { type = vp value = -50 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM073B" #Yes
		command = { type = infra value = 250 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -200 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Releasing mercenaries
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000079
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = 1
		atwar = no
		continent = europe
		NOT = { year = 1650 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM079" #Releasing mercenaries
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM079"
	#-#In times of peace, to save money, European states would release some of its mercenaries. This form of desertion was always used to cull the older aged troops.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM079A" #Release them
		command = { type = desertion which = -1 value = 5000 }
		command = { type = treasury value = 100 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM079B" #Status quo
		command = { type = treasury value = -20 }
		command = { type = land value = -200 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Great royal hunt
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96000080 #Paradox 1103
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = 1
		atwar = no
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM080" #Great royal hunt
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM080"
	#-#From time to time most rulers liked to arrange great royal hunts. These occasions were quite popular, but far from everyone were invited to participate - being invited to a royal hunt was a clear indication of favour. As with similar occasions, this was used by the King to diplomatically demonstrate his current favorites among the nobility as well as the foreign dignitaries.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 15 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -15 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 15 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -15 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = 15 }
		command = { type = relation which = -1 value = -15 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#Petition for Redress
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 91000082 #Paradox 1072
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		stability = -1
		NOT = { domestic = { type = centralization value = 10 } }
		countrysize = 4
		NOT = { countrysize = 9 }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM082" #Petition for Redress
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM082"
	#-#Peasants typically had no voice but they could occasionally gain access to the monarch and ask for redress. Sometimes, these requests for redress would be directed at the local lord who was perceived to be violating the peasants' rights. Stepping in to override a noble's local authority was a very drastic step.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM082A" #Accept Petition
		command = { type = stability value = -4 }
		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = 1 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM082B" #Deny Petition
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = provincetax which = -1 value = -1 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 93000082 #Paradox 1072
	trigger = {

		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}

		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM082B" #Accept Petition

		command = { type = domestic which = centralization value = 1 }
	}
}

#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
#New Religious Order Petition (Courtesy of Korath and Pierreluc)
#-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

event = {
	id = 96009087
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		ai = no
		stability = -2
		NOT = { stability = 3 }
		relation = { country = PAP data = -190 }
		continent = europe
		domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 }
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 10 } }
		OR = {
			religion = catholic
			religion = counterreform
		}
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM087" #Petition for a new religious order
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM087"
	#-#A devout prior has petitioned us to support a new religious order. Of course, virtue is not free, and a small bequest would reinforce our already widespread reputation for charity.

	action_a = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM087A" #Remind the prior of his vow of poverty
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = relation which = PAP value = -10 }
	}
	action_b = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM087B" #Support the monastic order
		command = { type = stability value = 1 }
		command = { type = treasury value = -50 }
		command = { type = relation which = PAP value = 25 }
		command = { type = missionaries value = 1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = -1 }
	}
	action_c = {
		name = "ACTIONNAME_RANDOM087C" #Forbid the order and banish the prior
		command = { type = stability value = -2 }
		command = { type = relation which = PAP value = -100 }
		command = { type = missionaries value = -1 }
		command = { type = domestic which = innovative value = 1 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96000090
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 4 } }
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM090" #Conversion by the Sword
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM090"
	#-#While often conversion to another faith was done by persuasion, sometimes zealous fanatics would get out of hand and demand conversion of a population or death.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = conversion which = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -3 value = -1000 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 96010090
	trigger = {
		NOT = { owned = { province = 1614 data = -1 } } #not for the Pope (MUS)
		NOT = { domestic = { type = innovative value = 2 } }
		NOT = { religion = confucian }
	}
	random = yes
	name = "EVENTNAME_RANDOM090" #Conversion by the Sword
	desc = "EVENTHIST_RANDOM090"
	#-#While often conversion to another faith was done by persuasion, sometimes zealous fanatics would get out of hand and demand conversion of a population or death.

	action_a = {
		name = "OK"
		command = { type = stability value = -1 }
		command = { type = conversion which = -1 }
		command = { type = population which = -3 value = -1000 }
		command = { type = revolt which = -3 }
	}
}
